<br>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">ITEM 2.01. Completion of Acquisition or Disposition of Assets.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">On&#160;July 24, 2015, pursuant to the Agreement and Plan of Merger, dated as of May 18, 2014 (the &#8220;Merger Agreement&#8221;), among DIRECTV (&#8220;DIRECTV&#8221;), AT&amp;T Inc. (&#8220;AT&amp;T&#8221;) and Steam Merger Sub LLC (now known as DIRECTV Group Holdings, LLC), a wholly owned subsidiary of AT&amp;T (&#8220;Merger Sub&#8221;), DIRECTV merged with and into Merger Sub, with Merger Sub being renamed DIRECTV Group Holdings, LLC and continuing as the surviving entity and as a direct wholly owned subsidiary of AT&amp;T (the &#8220;Merger&#8221;).</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">At the closing of the Merger, each outstanding share of DIRECTV common stock, par value $0.01 per share (&#8220;DIRECTV Common Stock&#8221;), was converted into the right to receive 1.892 shares of AT&amp;T common stock, par value $1.00 per share (&#8220;AT&amp;T Common Stock&#8221;) plus $28.50 in cash, and cash in lieu of any fractional shares. AT&amp;T issued approximately 954,541,877 shares of AT&amp;T Common Stock to former holders of DIRECTV Common Stock. Each outstanding option to purchase shares of DIRECTV Common Stock was converted into an option to acquire a number of shares of AT&amp;T Common Stock on the same terms and conditions as were applicable under such option immediately prior to the Merger, except that the exercise price and the number of shares of AT&amp;T Common Stock issuable upon exercise of such option were adjusted based on a ratio of 2.703 (the &#8220;Option Exchange Ratio&#8221;). Each outstanding stock appreciation right to receive shares of DIRECTV Common Stock or cash was converted into a stock appreciation right on shares of AT&amp;T Common Stock on the same terms and conditions as were applicable under such stock appreciation right immediately prior to the Merger, except that the reference price per share and the number of shares of AT&amp;T Common Stock subject to such stock appreciation right were adjusted based on the Option Exchange Ratio. Each restricted stock unit and performance stock unit of DIRECTV was converted into a restricted stock unit on a number of shares of AT&amp;T Common Stock on the same terms and conditions as were applicable under such restricted stock unit or performance stock unit immediately prior to the Merger (including any applicable dividend equivalent rights), except that the number of shares of AT&amp;T Common Stock underlying such restricted stock unit or performance stock unit was adjusted based on the Option Exchange Ratio.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font style="BACKGROUND-COLOR: #ffffff; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Based on the closing price of $34.29 per share of AT&amp;T Common Stock on the New York Stock Exchange on July 24, 2015, the aggregate implied value of the consideration paid to former holders of DIRECTV Common Stock in connection with the Merger was approximately $47.1 billion, including approximately $32.7 billion in AT&amp;T Common Stock and approximately $14.4 billion in cash.</font></font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">&#160;</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Upon the closing of the Merger, the DIRECTV Common Stock, which traded under the symbol &#8220;DTV&#8221;, ceased trading on, and is being delisted from, the NASDAQ Stock Market.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">The foregoing description of the Merger contained in this Item 2.01 does not purport to be complete and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the Merger Agreement, which is incorporated by reference as Exhibit 10.1 hereto and is incorporated by reference into this Item 2.01.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">ITEM 2.03. Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation under an Off-Balance Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">On July 24, 2015, in connection with the consummation of the Merger (as defined below), DIRECTV Holdings LLC and DIRECTV Financing Co., Inc. <div><br>
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Exhibit 4.1</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV HOLDINGS LLC</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV FINANCING CO., INC.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Second Supplemental Indenture</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">This Second Supplemental Indenture, dated as of&#160;July 24, 2015 (this &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Second Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), is entered into by and among DIRECTV Holdings LLC (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Company</font>&#8221; or an &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuer</font>&#8221;), a Delaware limited liability company, DIRECTV Financing Co., Inc. (&#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV Financing</font>&#8221; or an &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuer</font>&#8221; and together with the Company, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuers</font>&#8221;), a Delaware corporation, each of the Guarantors listed on the signature page hereto (together with any additional Subsidiary of the Company that becomes a Guarantor under the Indenture (as defined below) following the date hereof, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Guarantors</font>&#8221;), DIRECTV, a Delaware corporation (&#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV</font>&#8221; or the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Parent Guarantor</font>&#8221;), Steam Merger Sub LLC, a Delaware limited liability company (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">New Parent Guarantor</font>&#8221;) and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., a national banking association duly organized and existing under the laws of the United States, as Trustee (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trustee</font>&#8221;).</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">W I T N E S S E T H</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, under an indenture, dated as of September 22, 2009, as further amended and supplemented by the first supplemental indenture, dated as of November 14, 2011 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">First Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;) and as further amended and supplemented hereby (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Indenture</font>&#8221;), among the Issuers, the Guarantors and the Trustee, the Company has issued $1,000,000,000 of its 5.875% Senior Notes due 2019 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Notes</font>&#8221;);</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, Section 2(b)(ii) of the First Supplemental Indenture provides, among other things, that any Person to which Parent Guarantor&#8217;s sale, assignment, transfer, lease, conveyance, or other disposition of all or substantially all of its properties or assets shall not be deemed to be a successor to Parent Guarantor as a result of such transactions and will only become a Parent Guarantor if it elects to expressly assume the Guarantee of Parent Guarantor, and New Parent Guarantor hereby expressly elects to assume the Guarantee of Parent Guarantor;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, Section&#160;9.01 of the Indenture provides, among other things, that the Issuers, the Guarantors and the Trustee may amend the Indenture, the Notes of any Series and the Guarantees or any amended or supplemental indenture without the consent of any Holder of a Note &#8220;to provide for the assumption of the obligations of the Issuers or any Guarantors to the Holders of the Notes in the case of a merger or consolidation pursuant to Article 5 or Article 10 hereof&#8221;;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, DIRECTV is merging on the date hereof with and into the New Parent Guarantor pursuant to the terms of the Agreement and Plan or Merger, dated as of May 18, 2014, by and among DIRECTV, AT&amp;T Inc. and the New Parent Guarantor (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger Agreement</font>&#8221;), pursuant to which, at the Effective Time (as defined in the Merger Agreement) DIRECTV will merge with and into the New Parent Guarantor (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger</font>&#8221;), with the New Parent Guarantor as the surviving company and successor to the Parent Guarantor;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, pursuant to Article 10 of the Indenture, the Issuers, the Guarantors, the New Parent Guarantor, DIRECTV and the Trustee have entered into this Second Supplemental Indenture for the purposes stated herein;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, the Issuers have requested that the Trustee execute and deliver this Second Supplemental Indenture; and</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, the execution and delivery of this Second Supplemental Indenture has been duly authorized by the parties hereto, and all other acts and requirements necessary to make this Second Supplemental Indenture a valid and binding supplement to the Indenture effectively amending the Indenture as set forth herein have been duly taken.</font></div>

<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which are hereby acknowledged, the Issuers, the Guarantors, the New Parent Guarantor, DIRECTV and the Trustee mutually covenant and agree as follows:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Section 1.&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Definitions</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">As used in this Second Supplemental Indenture, terms defined in the Indenture or in the preamble or recital hereto are used herein as therein defined.&#160;&#160;The words &#8220;herein,&#8221; &#8220;hereof&#8221; and &#8220;hereby&#8221; and other words of similar import used in this Second Supplemental Indenture refer to this Second Supplemental Indenture as a whole and not to any particular Section hereof.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Section 2.&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Assumption</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(a)&#160;&#160;The New Parent Guarantor hereby assumes all obligations of the Parent Guarantor under the Indenture, the Notes and the Guarantees and shall succeed to and be substituted for the Parent Guarantor with the same effect as if the New Parent Guarantor had been named in the Indenture and the Guarantee as a Parent Guarantor.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(b)&#160;&#160;Section 2(a) shall become effective on the date hereof at the Effective Time.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Section 3.&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Miscellaneous</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(a)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ratification of Indenture</font>.&#160;&#160;All the provisions of this Second Supplemental Indenture shall be deemed to be incorporated in, and made a part of, the Indenture; and the Indenture, as supplemented and amended by this Second Supplemental Indenture, shall be read, taken and construed as one and the same instrument.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(b)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Headings</font>.&#160;&#160;The headings of the Sections of this Second Supplemental Indenture are inserted for convenience of information and reference and shall not be deemed to be a part thereof.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(c)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Counterparts</font>.&#160;&#160;This Second Supplemental Indenture may be executed in any number of counterparts each of which shall be an original; but such counterparts shall together constitute but one and the same instrument.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(d)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Conflict with Trust Indenture Act</font>.&#160;&#160;If any provision hereof limits, qualifies or conflicts with another provision hereof which is required to be included in this Second Supplemental Indenture by any of the provisions of the Trust Indenture Act, such required provision shall control.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(e)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Successors and Assigns</font>.&#160;&#160;All covenants and agreements in this Second Supplemental Indenture by the Company shall bind its successors and assigns, whether so expressed or not.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(f)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Separability</font>.&#160;&#160;In case any one or more of the provisions contained the Indenture or this Second Supplemental Indenture shall for any reason be held to be invalid, illegal or unenforceable in any respect, such invalidity, illegality or unenforceability shall not affect any other provisions of the Indenture or this Second Supplemental Indenture, but the Indenture or this Second Supplemental Indenture shall be construed as if such invalid or illegal or unenforceable provision had never been contained herein or therein.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 31.5pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(g)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Benefits of Second</font> <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Supplemental Indenture</font>.&#160;&#160;Nothing in this Second Supplemental Indenture, express or implied, shall give to any person, other than the parties hereto and their successors hereunder and the Holders, any benefit or any legal or equitable right, remedy, or claim under this Second Supplemental Indenture.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(h)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Trustee Not Responsible for Recitals</font>. The recitals and statements herein contained are made by the Issuers and the Guarantors and not by the Trustee, and the Trustee assumes no responsibility for the correctness thereof. The Trustee makes no representation as to the validity or sufficiency of this Second Supplemental Indenture.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV HOLDINGS LLC</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV FINANCING CO., INC.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Second Supplemental Indenture</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">This Second Supplemental Indenture, dated as of July 24, 2015 (this &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Second Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), is entered into by and among DIRECTV Holdings LLC (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Company</font>&#8221; or an &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuer</font>&#8221;), a Delaware limited liability company, DIRECTV Financing Co., Inc. (&#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV Financing</font>&#8221; or an &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuer</font>&#8221; and together with the Company, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuers</font>&#8221;), a Delaware corporation, each of the Guarantors listed on the signature page hereto (together with any additional Subsidiary of the Company that becomes a Guarantor under the Indenture (as defined below) following the date hereof, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Guarantors</font>&#8221;), DIRECTV, a Delaware corporation (&#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV</font>&#8221; or the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Parent Guarantor</font>&#8221;), Steam Merger Sub LLC, a Delaware limited liability company (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">New Parent Guarantor</font>&#8221;) and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., a national banking association duly organized and existing under the laws of the United States, as Trustee (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trustee</font>&#8221;).</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">W I T N E S S E T H</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, under an indenture, dated as of March 11, 2010, as further amended and supplemented by the First Supplemental Indenture, dated as of November 14, 2011 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">First Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;) and as further amended and supplemented hereby (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Indenture</font>&#8221;), among the Issuers, the Guarantors and the Trustee, the Company has issued $1,300,000,000 of its 5.200% Senior Notes due 2020 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">2020 Notes</font>&#8221;) and $500,000,000 of its 6.350% Senior Notes due 2040 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">2040 Notes</font>&#8221; and, together with the 2020 Notes, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Notes</font>&#8221;);&#160;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, Section 2(b)(ii) of the First Supplemental Indenture provides, among other things, that any Person to which Parent Guarantor&#8217;s sale, assignment, transfer, lease, conveyance, or other disposition of all or substantially all of its properties or assets shall not be deemed to be a successor to Parent Guarantor as a result of such transactions and will only become a Parent Guarantor if it elects to expressly assume the Guarantee of Parent Guarantor, and New Parent Guarantor hereby expressly elects to assume the Guarantee of Parent Guarantor;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, Section&#160;9.01 of the Indenture provides, among other things, that the Issuers, the Guarantors and the Trustee may amend the Indenture, the Notes of any Series and the Guarantees or any amended or supplemental indenture without the consent of any Holder of a Note &#8220;to provide for the assumption of the obligations of the Issuers or any Guarantors to the Holders of the Notes in the case of a merger or consolidation pursuant to Article 5 or Article 10 hereof&#8221;;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, DIRECTV is merging on the date hereof with and into the New Parent Guarantor pursuant to the terms of the Agreement and Plan or Merger, dated as of May 18, 2014, by and among DIRECTV, AT&amp;T Inc. and the New Parent Guarantor (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger Agreement</font>&#8221;), pursuant to which, at the Effective Time (as defined in the Merger Agreement) DIRECTV will merge with and into the New Parent Guarantor (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger</font>&#8221;), with the New Parent Guarantor as the surviving company and successor to the Parent Guarantor;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, pursuant to Article 10 of the Indenture, the Issuers, the Guarantors, the New Parent Guarantor, DIRECTV and the Trustee have entered into this Second Supplemental Indenture for the purposes stated herein;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, the Issuers have requested that the Trustee execute and deliver this Second Supplemental Indenture; and</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, the execution and delivery of this Second Supplemental Indenture has been duly authorized by the parties hereto, and all other acts and requirements necessary to make this Second Supplemental Indenture a valid and binding supplement to the Indenture effectively amending the Indenture as set forth herein have been duly taken.</font></div>

<br>
<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">

<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">&#160; </font></div>

<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">1</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which are hereby acknowledged, the Issuers, the Guarantors, the New Parent Guarantor, DIRECTV and the Trustee mutually covenant and agree as follows:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">&#160;Section 1.&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Definitions</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">As used in this Second Supplemental Indenture, terms defined in the Indenture or in the preamble or recital hereto are used herein as therein defined.&#160;&#160;The words &#8220;herein,&#8221; &#8220;hereof&#8221; and &#8220;hereby&#8221; and other words of similar import used in this Second Supplemental Indenture refer to this Second Supplemental Indenture as a whole and not to any particular Section hereof.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Section 2.&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Assumption</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(a)&#160;&#160;The New Parent Guarantor hereby assumes all obligations of the Parent Guarantor under the Indenture, the Notes and the Guarantees and shall succeed to and be substituted for the Parent Guarantor with the same effect as if the New Parent Guarantor had been named in the Indenture and the Guarantee as a Parent Guarantor.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(b)&#160;&#160;Section 2(a) shall become effective on the date hereof at the Effective Time.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Section 3.&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Miscellaneous</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(a)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ratification of Indenture</font>.&#160;&#160;All the provisions of this Second Supplemental Indenture shall be deemed to be incorporated in, and made a part of, the Indenture; and the Indenture, as supplemented and amended by this Second Supplemental Indenture, shall be read, taken and construed as one and the same instrument.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(b)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Headings</font>.&#160;&#160;The headings of the Sections of this Second Supplemental Indenture are inserted for convenience of information and reference and shall not be deemed to be a part thereof.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(c)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Counterparts</font>.&#160;&#160;This Second Supplemental Indenture may be executed in any number of counterparts each of which shall be an original; but such counterparts shall together constitute but one and the same instrument.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(d)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Conflict with Trust Indenture Act</font>.&#160;&#160;If any provision hereof limits, qualifies or conflicts with another provision hereof which is required to be included in this Second Supplemental Indenture by any of the provisions of the Trust Indenture Act, such required provision shall control.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(e)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Successors and Assigns</font>.&#160;&#160;All covenants and agreements in this Second Supplemental Indenture by the Company shall bind its successors and assigns, whether so expressed or not.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(f)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Separability</font>.&#160;&#160;In case any one or more of the provisions contained the Indenture or this Second Supplemental Indenture shall for any reason be held to be invalid, illegal or unenforceable in any respect, such invalidity, illegality or unenforceability shall not affect any other provisions of the Indenture or this Second Supplemental Indenture, but the Indenture or this Second Supplemental Indenture shall be construed as if such invalid or illegal or unenforceable provision had never been contained herein or therein.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 31.5pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(g)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Benefits of Second</font> <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Supplemental Indenture</font>.&#160;&#160;Nothing in this Second Supplemental Indenture, express or implied, shall give to any person, other than the parties hereto and their successors hereunder and the Holders, any benefit or any legal or equitable right, remedy, or claim under this Second Supplemental Indenture.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(h)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Trustee Not Responsible for Recitals</font>. The recitals and statements herein contained are made by the Issuers and the Guarantors and not by the Trustee, and the Trustee assumes no responsibility for the correctness thereof. The Trustee makes no representation as to the validity or sufficiency of this Second Supplemental Indenture.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV HOLDINGS LLC</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV FINANCING CO., INC.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Fifth Supplemental Indenture</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">This Fifth Supplemental Indenture, dated as of July 24, 2015 (this &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Fifth Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), is entered into by and among DIRECTV Holdings LLC (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Company</font>&#8221; or an &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuer</font>&#8221;), a Delaware limited liability company, DIRECTV Financing Co., Inc. (&#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV Financing</font>&#8221; or an &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuer</font>&#8221; and together with the Company, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuers</font>&#8221;), a Delaware corporation, each of the Guarantors listed on the signature page hereto (together with any additional Subsidiary of the Company that becomes a Guarantor under the Indenture (as defined below) following the date hereof, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Guarantors</font>&#8221;), DIRECTV, a Delaware corporation (&#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV</font>&#8221; or the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Parent Guarantor</font>&#8221;), Steam Merger Sub LLC, a Delaware limited liability company (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">New Parent Guarantor</font>&#8221;) and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., a national banking association duly organized and existing under the laws of the United States, as Trustee (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trustee</font>&#8221;).</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">W I T N E S S E T H</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, under an indenture, dated as of August 17, 2010 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Base Indenture</font>&#8221;), as amended and supplemented by the first supplemental indenture dated as of August 17, 2010 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">First Supplemental&#160;Indenture</font>&#8221;), as further amended and supplemented by the second supplemental indenture dated as of March 10, 2011 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Second Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), as further amended and supplemented by the third supplemental indenture dated as of November 14, 2011(the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Third Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), as further amended and supplemented by the fourth supplemental indenture dated as of November 14, 2011 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Fourth Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;) and as further amended and amended and supplemented hereby (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Indenture</font>&#8221;), the Company has issued $750,000,000 of its 3.125% Senior Notes due 2016 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">2016 Notes</font>&#8221;), $1,000,000,000 of its 4.600% Senior Notes due 2021 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">2021 Notes</font>&#8221;), $1,250,000,000 of its 6.000% Senior Notes due 2040 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">6.000% 2040 Notes</font>&#8221;), $1,500,000,000 of its 3.500% Senior Notes due 2016 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">3.500% 2016 Notes</font>&#8221;), $1,500,000,000 of its 5.000% Senior Notes due 2021 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">5.000% 2021 Notes</font>&#8221;) and $1,000,000,000 of its 6.375% Senior Notes due 2041 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">2041 Notes</font>&#8221; and, collectively with the 2016 Notes, the 2021 Notes, the 6.000% 2040 Notes, the 3.500% 2016 Notes and the 5.000% 2021 Notes, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Notes</font>&#8221;);&#160;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, Section 2(b)(ii) of the Third Supplemental Indenture provides, among other things, that any Person to which Parent Guarantor&#8217;s sale, assignment, transfer, lease, conveyance, or other disposition of all or substantially all of its properties or assets shall not be deemed to be a successor to Parent Guarantor as a result of such transactions and will only become a Parent Guarantor if it elects to expressly assume the Guarantee of Parent Guarantor, and New Parent Guarantor hereby expressly elects to assume the Guarantee of Parent Guarantor;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, Section&#160;2.13(a) of the First Supplemental Indenture and Second Supplemental Indenture provides, among other things, that the Issuers, the Guarantors and the Trustee may amend the Indenture, the Notes of any series and the Guarantees or any amended or supplemental indenture without the consent of any Holder of a Note &#8220;to provide for the assumption of the obligations of the Issuers or any Guarantors to the Holders of the Notes in the case of a merger or consolidation pursuant to Article V or Article XV of the Indenture&#8221;;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, DIRECTV is merging on the date hereof with and into the New Parent Guarantor pursuant to the terms of the Agreement and Plan or Merger, dated as of May 18, 2014, by and among DIRECTV, AT&amp;T Inc. and the New Parent Guarantor (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger Agreement</font>&#8221;), pursuant to which, at the Effective Time (as defined in the Merger Agreement) DIRECTV will merge with and into the New Parent Guarantor (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger</font>&#8221;), with the New Parent Guarantor as the surviving company and successor to the Parent Guarantor;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, pursuant to Article XV of the Indenture, the Issuers, the Guarantors, the New Parent Guarantor, DIRECTV and the Trustee have entered into this Fifth Supplemental Indenture for the purposes stated herein;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, the Issuers have requested that the Trustee execute and deliver this Fifth Supplemental Indenture; and</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, the execution and delivery of this Fifth Supplemental Indenture has been duly authorized by the parties hereto, and all other acts and requirements necessary to make this Fifth Supplemental Indenture a valid and binding supplement to the Indenture effectively amending the Indenture as set forth herein have been duly taken.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the foregoing and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which are hereby acknowledged, the Issuers, the Guarantors, the New Parent Guarantor, DIRECTV and the Trustee mutually covenant and agree as follows:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">&#160;Section 1.&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Definitions</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">As used in this Fifth Supplemental Indenture, terms defined in the Indenture or in the preamble or recital hereto are used herein as therein defined.&#160;&#160;The words &#8220;herein,&#8221; &#8220;hereof&#8221; and &#8220;hereby&#8221; and other words of similar import used in this Fifth Supplemental Indenture refer to this Fifth Supplemental Indenture as a whole and not to any particular Section hereof.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Section 2.&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Assumption</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(a)&#160;&#160;The New Parent Guarantor hereby assumes all obligations of the Parent Guarantor under the Indenture, the Notes and the Guarantees and shall succeed to and be substituted for the Parent Guarantor with the same effect as if the New Parent Guarantor had been named in the Indenture and the Guarantee as a Parent Guarantor.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(b)&#160;&#160;Section 2(a) shall become effective on the date hereof at the Effective Time.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">Section 3.&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Miscellaneous</font>.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(a)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ratification of Indenture</font>.&#160;&#160;All the provisions of this Fifth Supplemental Indenture shall be deemed to be incorporated in, and made a part of, the Indenture; and the Indenture, as supplemented and amended by this Fifth Supplemental Indenture, shall be read, taken and construed as one and the same instrument.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(b)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Headings</font>.&#160;&#160;The headings of the Sections of this Fifth Supplemental Indenture are inserted for convenience of information and reference and shall not be deemed to be a part thereof.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(c)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Counterparts</font>.&#160;&#160;This Fifth Supplemental Indenture may be executed in any number of counterparts each of which shall be an original; but such counterparts shall together constitute but one and the same instrument.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(d)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Conflict with Trust Indenture Act</font>.&#160;&#160;If any provision hereof limits, qualifies or conflicts with another provision hereof which is required to be included in this Fifth Supplemental Indenture by any of the provisions of the Trust Indenture Act, such required provision shall control.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(e)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Successors and Assigns</font>.&#160;&#160;All covenants and agreements in this Fifth Supplemental Indenture by the Company shall bind its successors and assigns, whether so expressed or not.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">(f)&#160;&#160; <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Separability</font>.&#160;&#160;In case any one or more of the provisions contained the Indenture or this Fifth Supplemental Indenture shall for any reason be held to be invalid, illegal or unenforceable in any respect, such invalidity, illegality or unenforceability shall not affect any other provisions of the Indenture or this Fifth Supplemental Indenture, but the Indenture or this Fifth Supplemental Indenture shall be construed as if such invalid or illegal or unenforceable provision had never been contained herein or therein.</font></div>

The Trustee makes no representation as to the validity or sufficiency of this Fifth Supplemental Indenture.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">This First Supplemental Indenture, dated as of July 24, 2015 (this &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">First Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), is entered into by and among DIRECTV Holdings LLC (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Company</font>&#8221; or an &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuer</font>&#8221;), a Delaware limited liability company, DIRECTV Financing Co., Inc. (&#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV Financing</font>&#8221; or an &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuer</font>&#8221; and together with the Company, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Issuers</font>&#8221;), a Delaware corporation, each of the Guarantors listed on the signature page hereto (together with any additional Subsidiary of the Company that becomes a Guarantor under the Indenture (as defined below) following the date hereof, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Guarantors</font>&#8221;), DIRECTV, a Delaware corporation (&#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">DIRECTV</font>&#8221; or the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Parent Guarantor</font>&#8221;), Steam Merger Sub LLC, a Delaware limited liability company (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">New Parent Guarantor</font>&#8221;) and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., a national banking association duly organized and existing under the laws of the United States, as Trustee (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trustee</font>&#8221;)</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">W I T N E S S E T H</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, under an indenture, dated as of March 8, 2012, as further amended and supplemented hereby (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Indenture</font>&#8221;), among the Issuers, the Guarantors and the Trustee, the Company has issued $1,250,000,000 of its 2.400% Senior Notes due 2017 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">2017 Notes</font>&#8221;), $1,500,000,000 of its 3.800% Senior Notes due 2022 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">2022 Notes</font>&#8221;), $1,250,000,000 of its 5.150% Senior Notes due 2042 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">2042 Notes</font>&#8221; and, collectively with the 2017 Notes and the 2022 Notes, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Notes</font>&#8221;);</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, Section 10.03 of the Indenture provides, among other things, that any Person to which Parent Guarantor&#8217;s sale, assignment, transfer, lease, conveyance, or other disposition of all or substantially all of its properties or assets shall not be deemed to be a successor to Parent Guarantor as a result of such transactions and will only become a Parent Guarantor if it elects to expressly assume the Guarantee of Parent Guarantor, and New Parent Guarantor hereby expressly elects to assume the Guarantee of Parent Guarantor;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, Section&#160;9.01 of the Indenture provides, among other things, that the Issuers, the Guarantors and the Trustee may amend the Indenture, the Notes of any Series and the Guarantees or any amended or supplemental indenture without the consent of any Holder of a Note &#8220;to provide for the assumption of the obligations of the Issuers or any Guarantors to the Holders of the Notes in the case of a merger or consolidation pursuant to Article 5 or Article 10 hereof&#8221;;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, DIRECTV wishes to merge on the date hereof with and into the New Parent Guarantor pursuant to the terms of the Agreement and Plan or Merger, dated as of May 18, 2014, by and among DIRECTV, AT&amp;T Inc. and the New Parent Guarantor (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger Agreement</font>&#8221;), pursuant to which, at the Effective Time (as defined in the Merger Agreement) DIRECTV will merge with and into the New Parent Guarantor (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger</font>&#8221;), with the New Parent Guarantor as the surviving company and successor to the Parent Guarantor;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, pursuant to Article 10 of the Indenture, the Issuers, the Guarantors, the New Parent Guarantor, DIRECTV and the Trustee have entered into this First Supplemental Indenture for the purposes stated herein;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, the Issuers have requested that the Trustee execute and deliver this First Supplemental Indenture; and</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 12pt">WHEREAS, the execution and delivery of this First Supplemental Indenture has been duly authorized by the parties hereto, and all other acts and requirements necessary to make this First Supplemental Indenture a valid and binding supplement to the Indenture effectively amending the Indenture as set forth herein have been duly taken.</font></div>
